If creating `data-validator.ext`, search for `*-validator.ext`\n   - Match naming conventions from the codebase\n\n3. **By architectural layer:**\n   - Controllers: `src/controllers/**/*.ext`\n   - Services: `src/services/**/*.ext`\n   -
